0.55 percent with carbon not exceeding 0.30 percent and manganese not exceeding 1.5 percent.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Comply with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JIS Z 3881<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> unless otherwise specified. Do not tack weld reinforcing bars.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Welded assemblies of steel reinforcement produced under factory conditions, such as welded wire reinforcement, bar mats, and deformed 
bar anchors, are allowed.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT></PRT><PRT outline="3"><TTL>PART 3 EXECUTION</TTL><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.1"><TTL>EXAMINATION</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Do not begin installation until substrates have been properly constructed; verify that substrates are level.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. If substrate preparation is the responsibility of another installer, notify Contracting Officer of unsatisfactory preparation before 
processing.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Check field dimensions before beginning installation. If dimensions vary too much from design dimensions for proper installation, 
notify Contracting Officer and wait for instructions before beginning installation.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.2"><TTL>PREPARATION</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Options for uses of excess concrete include: additional paving, post footing anchorage, swale riprap reinforcing, 
mud slab, flowable fill, footing bottom, retaining wall footing ballast, storm structure covers, underground utility 
pipe kickers, storm pipe flared end section, toe wash protection, and shoulder and toe outfall restraints for 
temporary erosion pipes. Diverting waste from the landfill contributes to the following LEED credit: MR2. Coordinate 
with Section <SRF><pre class="display_SRF">&lt;SRF&gt;</pre>01 33 29<pre class="display_SRF">&lt;/SRF&gt;</pre></SRF> SUSTAINABILITY REPORTING.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Determine quantity of concrete needed and minimize the production of excess concrete. Designate locations or uses for potential excess concrete 
before the concrete is poured.</TXT><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.2.1"><TTL>General</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Surfaces against which concrete is to be placed must be free of debris, loose material, standing water, snow, ice, and other deleterious 
substances before start of concrete placing.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Remove standing water without washing over freshly deposited concrete. Divert flow of water through side drains provided for such purpose.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.2.2"><TTL>Subgrade Under Foundations and Footings</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. When subgrade material is semi-porous and dry, sprinkle subgrade surface with water as required to eliminate suction at the time concrete 
is deposited, or seal subgrade surface by covering surface with specified vapor retarder.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. When subgrade material is porous, seal subgrade surface by covering surface with specified vapor retarder.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.2.3"><TTL>Subgrade Under Slabs on Ground</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Before construction of slabs on ground, have underground work on pipes and conduits completed and approved.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Previously constructed subgrade or fill must be cleaned of foreign materials</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Finish surface of capillary water barrier under interior slabs on ground must not show deviation in excess of<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 6 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1/4 inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> when tested 
with a<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 3000 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 10-foot<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> straightedge parallel with and at right angles to building lines.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">d. Finished surface of subgrade or fill under exterior slabs on ground must not be more than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 6 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 0.02-foot<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> above or<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 30 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 0.10-foot<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> below 
elevation indicated.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.2.4"><TTL>Edge Forms and Screed Strips for Slabs</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Set edge forms or bulkheads and intermediate screed strips for slabs to obtain indicated elevations and contours in finished slab surface 
and must be strong enough to support vibrating bridge screeds or roller pipe screeds if nature of specified slab finish requires use of 
such equipment.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Align concrete surface to elevation of screed strips by use of strike-off templates or approved compacting-type screeds.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.2.5"><TTL>Reinforcement and Other Embedded Items</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Secure reinforcement, joint materials, and other embedded materials in position, inspected, and approved before start of concrete placing.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. When concrete is placed, reinforcement must be free of materials deleterious to bond. Reinforcement with rust, mill scale, or a combination 
of both will be considered satisfactory, provided minimum nominal dimensions, nominal weight, and minimum average height of deformations 
of a hand-wire-brushed test specimen are not less than applicable ASTM specification requirements.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.3"><TTL>FORMS</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: For more information on formwork construction and best practices refer to ACI SP-004 "Formwork for Concrete" 
or ACI 347R "Guide to Formwork for Concrete".<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Provide forms, shoring, and scaffolding for concrete placement. Set forms mortar-tight and true to line and grade.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Chamfer above grade exposed joints, edges, and external corners of concrete<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> <div class="brackets">[20 mm]</div><pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> <div class="brackets">[0.75 inch]</div><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>. Place chamfer strips in corners of 
formwork to produce beveled edges on permanently exposed surfaces.<div class="brackets">[ Do not bevel reentrant corners or edges of formed joints of concrete.]</div></LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Provide formwork with clean-out openings to permit inspection and removal of debris.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">d. Inspect formwork and remove foreign material before concrete is placed.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">e. At construction joints, lap form-facing materials over the concrete of previous placement. Ensure formwork is placed against hardened 
concrete so offsets at construction joints conform to specified tolerances.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">f. Provide positive means of adjustment (such as wedges or jacks) of shores and struts. Do not make adjustments in formwork after concrete 
has reached initial setting. Brace formwork to resist lateral deflection and lateral instability.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">g. Fasten form wedges in place after final adjustment of forms and before concrete placement.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">h. Provide anchoring and bracing to control upward and lateral movement of formwork system.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">i. Construct formwork for openings to facilitate removal and to produce opening dimensions as specified and within tolerances.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">j. Provide runways for moving equipment. Support runways directly on formwork or structural members. Do not support runways on reinforcement. 
Loading applied by runways must not exceed capacity of formwork or structural members.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">k. Position and support expansion joint materials, waterstops, and other embedded items to prevent displacement. Fill voids in sleeves, 
inserts, and anchor slots temporarily with removable material to prevent concrete entry into voids.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">l. Clean surfaces of formwork and embedded materials of mortar, grout, and foreign materials before concrete placement.</LST><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.3.1"><TTL>Coating</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Coating forms with a film-forming material such as epoxy or polyurethane, along with the use of a proper 
release agent, will make stripping easier and allow more reuses of the forms. It is important however to not 
allow the release agent to reach the reinforcement because it would hinder the formation of a bond between concrete 
and the reinforcement.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Cover formwork surfaces with an acceptable material that inhibits bond with concrete.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. If formwork release agent is used, apply to formwork surfaces in accordance with manufacturer's recommendations before placing reinforcement. 
Remove excess release agent on formwork prior to concrete placement.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Do not allow formwork release agent to contact reinforcement or hardened concrete against which fresh concrete is to be placed.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.3.2"><TTL>Reshoring</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Reshores, as defined in ACI 347R, are shores placed snugly under a stripped concrete slab or other structural 
member after the original forms and shores have been removed from a full bay, requiring the new slab or structural 
member to deflect and support its own weight and existing construction loads applied before installation of the 
reshores. Such reshores are provided to transfer additional construction loads to other slabs or members and/or 
to impede deflection due to creep that might otherwise occur.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Do not allow structural members to be loaded with combined dead and construction loads in excess of loads indicated in the accepted 
procedure.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Install and remove reshores or backshores in accordance with accepted procedure.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. For floors supporting shores under newly placed concrete, either leave original supporting shores in place, or install reshores or 
backshores. Shoring system and supporting slabs must resist anticipated loads. Locate reshores and backshores directly under a shore 
position or as indicated on formwork shop drawings.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">d. In multistory buildings, place reshoring or backshoring over a sufficient number of stories to distribute weight of newly placed concrete, 
forms, and construction live loads.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.3.3"><TTL>Reuse</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Reuse forms providing the structural integrity of concrete and the aesthetics of exposed concrete are not compromised.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Wood forms must not be clogged with paste and must be capable of absorbing high water-cementitious material ratio paste.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Remove leaked mortar from formwork joints before reuse.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.3.4"><TTL>Forms for Standard Rough Form Finish</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: According to ACI 301, surface finish-1.0 (SF-1.0) has the following requirements:<BRK />
(a) No formwork facing material is specified<BRK />
(b) Patch voids larger than 40mm wide or 13mm deep<BRK />
(c) Remove projections larger than 25mm<BRK />
(d) Tie holes need not be patched<BRK />
(e) Surface tolerance Class D as specified in ACI 117<BRK />
(f) Mockup not required<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Provide formwork in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> with a surface finish, <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> SF-1.0, for formed surfaces that are to be concealed 
by other construction.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.3.5"><TTL>Forms for Standard Smooth Form Finish</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: When exposed to view, formed surfaces require a special architectural finish such as textured form finishes, 
sculptured inserts, special panel finish, and aggregate transfer finish. Requirements for such formwork must 
be specified. Select bracketed line for no mockup of the form finish otherwise mockup is required per ACI 301.<BRK />
According to ACI 301, surface finish-3.0 (SF-3.0) has the following requirements:<BRK />
(a) Patch voids larger than 20mm wide or 13mm deep<BRK />
(b) Remove projections larger than 3mm.<BRK />
(c) Patch tie holes<BRK />
(d) Surface tolerance Class A as specified in ACI 117<BRK />
(e) Provide mockup of concrete surface appearance and texture<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>Pan-joist forms is likely not available in Japan, therefore paragraph will be deleted.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Provide formwork in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> with a surface finish, <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> SF-3.0, for formed surfaces that are exposed to 
view.<div class="brackets">[ Do not provide mockup of concrete surface appearance and texture.]</div></TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.3.6"><TTL>Form Ties</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. For post-tensioned structures, do not remove formwork supports until stressing records have been accepted by the Contracting Officer.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. After ends or end fasteners of form ties have been removed, repair tie holes in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.3.7"><TTL>Tolerances for Form Construction</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Construct formwork so concrete surfaces conform to tolerances in <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Position and secure sleeves, inserts, anchors, and other embedded items such that embedded items are positioned within <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>
 tolerances.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. To maintain specified elevation and thickness within tolerances, install formwork to compensate for deflection and anticipated settlement 
in formwork during concrete placement. Set formwork and intermediate screed strips for slabs to produce designated elevation, camber, 
and contour of finished surface before formwork removal. If specified finish requires use of vibrating screeds or roller pipe screeds, 
ensure that edge forms and screed strips are strong enough to support such equipment.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.3.8"><TTL>Removal of Forms and Supports</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. If vertical formed surfaces require finishing, remove forms as soon as removal operations will not damage concrete.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Remove top forms on sloping surfaces of concrete as soon as removal will not allow concrete to sag. Perform repairs and finishing 
operations required. If forms are removed before end of specified curing period, provide curing and protection.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Do not damage concrete during removal of vertical formwork for columns, walls, and sides of beams. Perform needed repair and finishing 
operations required on vertical surfaces. If forms are removed before end of specified curing period, provide curing and protection.</LST><BRK />
<div class="brackets">[<LST INDENT="-0.33">d. Leave formwork and shoring in place to support construction loads and weight of concrete in beams, slabs, and other structural members 
until in-place required strength of concrete is reached.</LST><BRK />
]</div><LST INDENT="-0.33">e. Form-facing material and horizontal facing support members may be removed before in-place concrete reaches specified compressive strength 
if shores and other supports are designed to allow facing removal without deflection of supported slab or member.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.3.9"><TTL>Strength of Concrete Required for Removal of Formwork</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Supporting forms and shores should not be removed from beams, floors, and walls until these structural 
units are strong enough to carry their own weight and any approved super-imposed load. In no case should supporting 
forms and shores be removed from horizontal members before the concrete has achieved the specified stripping strength. 
Shores supporting post-tensioned construction should not be removed until sufficient tensioning force is applied 
to support the dead load, formwork, and anticipated construction loads.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>If removal of formwork, reshoring, or backshoring is based on concrete reaching a specified in-place strength, mold and field-cure cylinders in 
accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JIS A 1132<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>. Test cylinders in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JIS A 1108<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>. </TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.4"><TTL>WATERSTOP INSTALLATION AND SPLICES</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Provide waterstops in construction joints as indicated.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Install formwork to accommodate waterstop materials. Locate waterstops in joints where indicated in Contract Documents. Minimize 
number of splices in waterstop. Splice waterstops in accordance with manufacturer's written instructions. Install factory-manufactured 
premolded mitered corners.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Install waterstops to form a continuous diaphragm in each joint. Make adequate provisions to support and protect waterstops during 
progress of work. Protect waterstops protruding from joints from damage.</LST><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.4.1"><TTL>PVC Waterstop</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Make splices by heat sealing the adjacent waterstop edges together using a thermoplastic splicing iron utilizing a non-stick surface specifically 
designed for waterstop welding. Reform waterstops at splices with a remolding iron with ribs or corrugations to match the pattern of the waterstop. 
The spliced area, when cooled, must show no signs of separation, holes, or other imperfections when bent by hand in as sharp an angle as possible.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.4.2"><TTL>Rubber Waterstop</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Rubber waterstops must be spliced using cold bond adhesive as recommended by the manufacturer.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.4.3"><TTL>Thermoplastic Elastomeric Rubber Waterstop</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Fittings must be shop made using a machine specifically designed to mechanically weld the waterstop. A portable power saw must be used to miter 
or straight cut the ends to be joined to ensure good alignment and contact between joined surfaces. Maintain continuity of the characteristic 
features of the cross section of the waterstop (for example ribs, tabular center axis, and protrusions) across the splice.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.4.4"><TTL>Hydrophilic Waterstop</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Miter cut ends to be joined with sharp knife or shears. The ends must be adhered with adhesive.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.5"><TTL>PLACING REINFORCEMENT AND MISCELLANEOUS MATERIALS</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Unless otherwise specified, placing reinforcement and miscellaneous materials must be in accordance to <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>
. Provide bars, welded wire reinforcement, wire ties, supports, and other devices necessary to install and secure reinforcement.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Reinforcement must not have rust, scale, oil, grease, clay, or foreign substances that would reduce the bond. Rusting of reinforcement 
is a basis of rejection if the effective cross-sectional area or the nominal weight per unit length has been reduced. Remove loose rust 
prior to placing steel. Tack welding is prohibited.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Nonprestressed cast-in-place concrete members must have concrete cover for reinforcement given in the following table:</LST><BRK />
<HL4><TAB WIDTH="82">

<BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL />
<BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL />
<BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /><BRL /></TAB></HL4><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.5.1"><TTL>General</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Provide details of reinforcement that are in accordance with the Contract Documents.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.2"><TTL>Vapor Retarder <div class="brackets">[and Vapor Barrier]</div></TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Locate vapor retarder below the slab-on-grade per ACI 360R, figure 4-7. Refer to ASTM<BRK />
E1643 for standard practice and procedures for selecting, designing, installing and inspecting<BRK />
flexible, prefabricated sheet membranes used as vapor retarders/barriers under concrete slabs<BRK />
and edit/amend paragraph 3.5.2 as required.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Level and compact base material and install vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> with the longest dimension parallel with the direction of 
concrete pour and face laps away from direction of pour whenever possible. Extend vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> over footings, and seal 
to foundation wall, grade beam, or slab at an elevation consistent with the top of the slab or terminate at impediments such as dowels 
or water stops. Seal around all penetrations such as utilities and columns with vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> material and seal tape. 
Use the greatest widths and lengths practicable to eliminate joints wherever possible. Lap joints a minimum of 300 mm and tape. <div class="brackets">[Extend 
vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> over the tops of pile caps and grade beams to a distance acceptable to the contracting officer and terminate 
as recommended by the manufacturer.]</div></LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Protect vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> from damage during installation of reinforcing steel, utilities and concrete. Provide reinforcing 
bar supports with base section that minimize the potential for puncture of vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div>. Avoid use of stakes driven through 
the vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div>.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Inspect installation of vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> including sealing of joints and penetrations and mark all areas of damage and 
insufficient installation in advance of concrete placement such that deficiencies are corrected before concrete is placed. Remove torn, 
punctured or damaged vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> and repair damaged areas prior to concrete placement with vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> 
material lapped and sealed a minimum of 150 mm beyond damaged area or as instructed by the manufacturer.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33"><div class="brackets">[d. Place a 50 mm layer of clean concrete sand on vapor retarder <div class="brackets">[vapor barrier]</div> before placing concrete.]</div></LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.3"><TTL>Perimeter Insulation</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: When this paragraph is used, ensure that drawings indicate location and extent of perimeter insulation.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Install perimeter insulation at locations indicated. Adhesive must be used where insulation is applied to the interior surface of foundation walls 
and may be used for exterior application.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.4"><TTL>Reinforcement Supports</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: ACI 301 requirements have change for welded wire reinforcement support. If reinforcement less than W4.0 
or D4.0 is specified, the continuous support spacing should be less than or equal to<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 30 cm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 12 in<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Provide reinforcement support in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>. Supports for coated or galvanized bars must also be coated with 
electrically compatible material for a distance of at least<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 50 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 2 inches<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> beyond the point of contact with the bars.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.5"><TTL>Splicing</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>Splice lengths should be specified by Engineer of Record in the Contract Documents. JASS 5 and MLIT Standard Specification, 
Chapter 6 splice lengths does not meet ACI 318 requirements.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Lap slice lengths and locations as indicated in the Contract Documents. For splice locations not indicated follow <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>
, at no additional cost to the Government and subject to approval. Splicing must be by lapping, by gas pressure welding, or by mechanical or welded 
connection, except that lap splices must not be used for bars larger than D35. Do not splice at points of maximum stress and stagger splices a 
minimum of <div class="brackets">[600]</div><div class="brackets">[1200]</div><div class="brackets">[_____]</div> mm or as otherwise indicated so no more than half of the bars are spliced at any one section. </TXT><BRK />
<TXT>Overlap welded wire reinforcement the spacing of the cross wires, plus<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 50 mm. <pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET></TXT> <BRK />
<TXT>Approve welded splices prior to use.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.6"><TTL>Future Bonding</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Plug exposed, threaded, mechanical reinforcement bar connectors with a greased bolt. Provide bolt threads that match the connector. Countersink 
the connector in the concrete. Caulk the depression after the bolt is installed.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.7"><TTL>Setting Miscellaneous Material</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Place and secure anchors and bolts, pipe sleeves, conduits, and other such items in position before concrete placement and support against displacement. 
Plumb anchor bolts and check location and elevation. Temporarily fill voids in sleeves with readily removable material to prevent the entry of 
concrete.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.8"><TTL>Fabrication</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: JASS 5 and MLIT Standard specification, Chapter 6 requirements for hooks and bends does not fully meet 
ACI 318 and therefore Engineer of Record shall include details/dimensions for hooks and bends in the Contract 
Documents.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<TXT>Shop fabricate reinforcing bars to conform to shapes and dimensions indicated for reinforcement, and as follows:</TXT><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Provide fabrication tolerances that are in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Provide hooks and bends that are in accordance with the Contract Documents.</LST><BRK />
<TXT>Reinforcement must be bent cold to shapes as indicated. Bending must be done in the shop. Rebending of a reinforcing bar that has been bent incorrectly 
is not be permitted. Bending must be in accordance with standard approved practice and by approved machine methods.</TXT><BRK />
<TXT>Deliver reinforcing bars bundled, tagged, and marked. Tags must be metal with bar size, length, mark, and other information pressed in by machine. 
Marks must correspond with those used on the placing drawings.</TXT><BRK />
<TXT>Do not use reinforcement that has any of the following defects:</TXT><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Bar lengths, depths, and bends beyond specified fabrication tolerances</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Bends or kinks not indicated on drawings or approved shop drawings</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Bars with reduced cross-section due to rusting or other cause</LST><BRK />
<TXT>Replace defective reinforcement with new reinforcement having required shape, form, and cross-section area.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.9"><TTL>Placing Reinforcement</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Place reinforcement in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>.</TXT><BRK />
<TXT>For slabs on grade (over earth or over capillary water barrier) and for footing reinforcement, support bars or welded wire reinforcement on precast 
concrete blocks, spaced at intervals required by size of reinforcement, to keep reinforcement the minimum height specified above the underside 
of slab or footing.</TXT><BRK />
<TXT>For slabs other than on grade, supports for which any portion is less than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 25 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1 inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> from concrete surfaces that are exposed to view or to be 
painted must be of precast concrete units, plastic-coated steel, or stainless steel protected bar supports. Precast concrete units must be wedge 
shaped, not larger than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 90 by 90 mm,<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 3-1/2 by 3-1/2 inches,<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> and of thickness equal to that indicated for concrete protection of reinforcement. 
Provide precast units that have cast-in galvanized tie wire hooked for anchorage and blend with concrete surfaces after finishing is completed.</TXT><BRK />
<TXT>Provide reinforcement that is supported and secured together to prevent displacement by construction loads or by placing of wet concrete, and as 
follows:</TXT><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Provide supports for reinforcing bars that are sufficient in number and have sufficient strength to carry the reinforcement they support, 
and in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>. Do not use supports to support runways for concrete conveying equipment and similar 
construction loads.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Equip supports on ground and similar surfaces with sand-plates.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Support welded wire reinforcement as required for reinforcing bars.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">d. Secure reinforcements to supports by means of tie wire. Wire must be black, soft iron wire, not less than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 1.6 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 16 gage<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">e. Reinforcement must be accurately placed, securely tied at intersections, and held in position during placing of concrete by spacers, 
chairs, or other approved supports. Point wire-tie ends away from the form. Unless otherwise indicated, numbers, type, and spacing of 
supports must conform to the Contract Documents.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">f. Bending of reinforcing bars partially embedded in concrete is permitted only as specified in the Contract Documents.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.10"><TTL>Spacing of Reinforcing Bars</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Spacing must be as indicated in the Contract Documents.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Reinforcing bars may be relocated to avoid interference with other reinforcement, or with conduit, pipe, or other embedded items. 
If any reinforcing bar is moved a distance exceeding one bar diameter or specified placing tolerance, resulting rearrangement of reinforcement 
is subject to preapproval by the Contracting Officer.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.11"><TTL>Concrete Protection for Reinforcement</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: If the required concrete protection for reinforcement is greater than the thicknesses specified in the 
ACI building code requirements for reinforced concrete, (such as in extremely corrosive atmospheres or other severe 
exposures, for fire protection covering, and for concrete surface to receive exposed aggregate or tooled finish), 
such concrete protection for reinforcement must be indicated in the Contract Documents. ACI 201.2R and ACI 303R 
require additional concrete protection for severe exposure conditions. Also, refer to ACI 515.2R "Guide to Selecting 
Protective Treatments for Concrete" for more information about providing additional protection to concrete and 
reinforcing steel.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Additional concrete protection must be in accordance with the Contract Documents.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.5.12"><TTL>Welding</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Gas pressure welded connection splices is commonly used in Japan and therefore is specified. If other welding 
methods are utilized it shall follow AWS D1.4 or Jass 5. <pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Welding must be in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>. Welders shall be certified in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JIS Z 3881<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> for gas pressure welding. Welded joint connections 
shall develop 125 percent of the specified yield strength of the reinforcing bar and 100 percent of the specified tensile strength of the reinforcing 
bar.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.6"><TTL>BATCHING, MEASURING, MIXING, AND TRANSPORTING CONCRETE</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>In accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JIS A 5308<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>, <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>, except as modified herein. Batching equipment must be such that the concrete ingredients 
are consistently measured within the following tolerances: 1 percent for cement and water, 2 percent for aggregate, and 3 percent for admixtures. 
Furnish mandatory batch ticket information for each load of ready mix concrete.</TXT><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.6.1"><TTL>Measuring</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Make measurements at intervals as specified in paragraphs SAMPLING and TESTING.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.6.2"><TTL>Mixing</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Mix concrete in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JIS A 5308<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>, <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>. </LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Machine mix concrete. Begin mixing within 30 minutes after the cement has been added to the aggregates. Place concrete within 90 minutes 
of either addition of mixing water to cement and aggregates or addition of cement to aggregates if the air temperature is less than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 29 
degrees C<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 84 degrees F<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Reduce mixing time and place concrete within 60 minutes if the air temperature is greater than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 29 degrees C<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 84 degrees F<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> except as 
follows: if set retarding admixture is used and slump requirements can be met, limit for placing concrete may remain at 90 minutes. Additional 
water may be added, provided that both the specified maximum slump and submitted water-cementitious material ratio are not exceeded and 
the required concrete strength is still met. When additional water is added, an additional 30 revolutions of the mixer at mixing speed 
is required.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">d. <div class="brackets">[If the entrained air content falls below the specified limit, add a sufficient quantity of admixture to bring the entrained air content 
within the specified limits. ]</div>Dissolve admixtures in the mixing water and mix in the drum to uniformly distribute the admixture throughout 
the batch. Do not reconstitute concrete that has begun to solidify.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.6.3"><TTL>Transporting</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Transport concrete from the mixer to the forms as rapidly as practicable. Prevent segregation or loss of ingredients. Clean transporting equipment 
thoroughly before each batch. Do not use aluminum pipe or chutes. Remove concrete which has segregated in transporting and dispose of as directed.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.7"><TTL>PLACING CONCRETE</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: When necessary to deposit concrete under water use specifications <SRF><pre class="display_SRF">&lt;SRF&gt;</pre>03 31 30<pre class="display_SRF">&lt;/SRF&gt;</pre></SRF> MARINE CONCRETE.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Place concrete in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>.</TXT><BRK />
<div class="brackets">[<SPT outline="3.7.1"><TTL>Footing Placement</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Concrete for footings may be placed in excavations without forms upon inspection and approval by the Contracting Officer. Excavation width must 
be a minimum of<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 100 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 4 inches<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> greater than indicated.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
]</div><div class="brackets">[<SPT outline="3.7.2"><TTL>Pumping</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Pumping, especially lightweight concrete, requires careful attention to mix designs and pumping procedures. 
Allow pumping when other means of placement are impractical or more expensive.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT><RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>. Pumping must not result in separation or loss of materials nor cause interruptions sufficient to permit loss of 
plasticity between successive increments. Loss of slump in pumping equipment must not exceed<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 50 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 2 inches<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> at discharge/placement. Do not convey 
concrete through pipe made of aluminum or aluminum alloy. Avoid rapid changes in pipe sizes. Limit maximum size of course aggregate to 33 percent 
of the diameter of the pipe. Limit maximum size of well-rounded aggregate to 40 percent of the pipe diameter. Take samples for testing at both 
the point of delivery to the pump and at the discharge end.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
]</div><SPT outline="3.7.3"><TTL>Cold Weather</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: The major difference between ACI 301 and ACI 306.1 is that ACI 306.1 requires the contractor to submit 
detailed procedures (a plan) for cold weather concrete.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Cold weather concrete must meet the requirements of <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> unless otherwise specified. Do not allow concrete temperature 
to decrease below<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 10 degrees C<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 50 degrees F<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>. Obtain approval prior to placing concrete when the ambient temperature is below<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 4 degrees C<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 40 degrees 
F<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> or when concrete is likely to be subjected to freezing temperatures within 24 hours. Cover concrete and provide sufficient heat to maintain<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 
10 degrees C<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 50 degrees F<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> minimum adjacent to both the formwork and the structure while curing. Limit the rate of cooling to<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 3 degrees C<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 37 degrees 
F<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> in any 1 hour and<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 10 degrees C<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 50 degrees F<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> per 24 hours after heat application.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.7.4"><TTL>Hot Weather</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: The major difference between ACI 301 and ACI 305.1 is that ACI 305.1 requires the contractor to submit 
detailed procedures (a plan) for hot weather concrete.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT><div class="brackets">[Hot weather concrete must meet the requirements of <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> unless otherwise specified. ]</div>Maintain required concrete temperature 
using Figure 4.2 in <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 305R<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> to prevent the evaporation rate from exceeding<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 1 kg per square meter<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 0.2 pound of water per square foot<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> of exposed 
concrete per hour. Cool ingredients before mixing or use other suitable means to control concrete temperature and prevent rapid drying of newly 
placed concrete. Shade the fresh concrete as soon as possible after placing. Start curing when the surface of the fresh concrete is sufficiently 
hard to permit curing without damage. Provide water hoses, pipes, spraying equipment, and water hauling equipment, where job site is remote to 
water source, to maintain a moist concrete surface throughout the curing period. Provide burlap cover or other suitable, permeable material with 
fog spray or continuous wetting of the concrete when weather conditions prevent the use of either liquid membrane curing compound or impervious 
sheets. For vertical surfaces, protect forms from direct sunlight and add water to top of structure once concrete is set.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.7.5"><TTL>Bonding</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Surfaces of set concrete at joints, must be roughened and cleaned of laitance, coatings, loose particles, and foreign matter. Roughen surfaces 
in a manner that exposes the aggregate uniformly and does not leave laitance, loosened particles of aggregate, nor damaged concrete at the surface.</TXT><BRK />
<TXT>Obtain bonding of fresh concrete that has set as follows:</TXT><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. At joints between footings and walls or columns, between walls or columns and the beams or slabs they support, and elsewhere unless 
otherwise specified; roughened and cleaned surface of set concrete must be dampened, but not saturated, immediately prior to placing of 
fresh concrete.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. At joints in exposed-to-view work; at vertical joints in walls; at joints near midpoint of span in girders, beams, supported slabs, 
other structural members; in work designed to contain liquids; the roughened and cleaned surface of set concrete must be dampened but not 
saturated and covered with a cement grout coating.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Provide cement grout that consists of equal parts of portland cement and fine aggregate by weight with not more than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 22.5 liters<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 6 
gallons<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> of water per sack of cement. Apply cement grout with a stiff broom or brush to a minimum thickness of<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 1.6 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1/16 inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>. Deposit 
fresh concrete before cement grout has attained its initial set.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.8"><TTL>WASTE MANAGEMENT</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Provide as specified in the Waste Management Plan and as follows.</TXT><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.8.1"><TTL>Mixing Equipment</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Before concrete pours, designate<div class="brackets">[ Contractor-owned site meeting environmental standards]</div><div class="brackets">[ on-site area to be paved later in project]</div> for cleaning 
out concrete mixing trucks. Minimize water used to wash equipment.</TXT><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: The use of crushed waste concrete as an aggregate in the production of new concrete should follow the recommendations 
of ACI 555R.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.8.2"><TTL>Hardened, Cured Waste Concrete</TTL><BRK />
<TXT><div class="brackets">[Crush and reuse hardened, cured waste concrete as fill or as a base course for pavement. ]</div><div class="brackets">[Use hardened, cured waste concrete as aggregate in 
concrete mix if approved by Contracting Officer.]</div></TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.8.3"><TTL>Reinforcing Steel</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Collect reinforcing steel and place in designated area for recycling.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.8.4"><TTL>Other Waste</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Identify concrete manufacturer's or supplier's policy for collection or return of construction waste, unused material, deconstruction waste, and/or 
packaging material.<div class="brackets">[ Return excess cement to supplier.]</div><div class="brackets">[ Institute deconstruction and construction waste separation and recycling for use in 
manufacturer's programs. When such a program is not available, seek local recyclers to reclaim the materials.]</div></TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.9"><TTL>SURFACE FINISHES EXCEPT FLOOR, SLAB, AND PAVEMENT FINISHES</TTL><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.9.1"><TTL>Defects</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Repair surface defects in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.9.2"><TTL>Not Against Forms (Top of Walls)</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Surfaces not otherwise specified must be finished with wood floats to even surfaces. Finish must match adjacent finishes.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.9.3"><TTL>Formed Surfaces</TTL><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.9.3.1"><TTL>Tolerances</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Tolerances in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and as indicated.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.9.3.2"><TTL>As-Cast Rough Form</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Provide for surfaces not exposed to public view a surface finish SF-1.0. Patch holes and defects in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> or <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>
.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.9.3.3"><TTL>Standard Smooth Finish</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Provide for surfaces exposed to public view a surface finish SF-3.0. Patch holes and defects in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> or <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>
.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.9.4"><TTL><div class="brackets">[Smooth-Rubbed]</div><div class="brackets">[Grout-Cleaned Rubbed]</div><div class="brackets">[Cork-Floated]</div><div class="brackets">[Exposed Aggregate]</div> Finish</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Add information where special type of finish is desired. See ACI 301 for information on smooth rubbed 
finish, grout cleaned finish, cork floated finish, and exposed aggregate. Areas requiring special finish should 
be clearly indicated on the drawings and coordinated with the specifications.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT><div class="brackets">[Provide a smooth-rubbed finish per <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 5 in the locations indicated.]</div><div class="brackets">[Provide a grout-cleaned rubbed finish per <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 5 
in the locations indicated.]</div><div class="brackets">[Provide a cork-floated finish per <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 5 in the locations indicated.]</div><div class="brackets">[Provide an exposed aggregate finish 
per <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 5 in the locations indicated.]</div></TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.10"><TTL>FLOOR, SLAB, AND PAVEMENT FINISHES AND MISCELLANEOUS CONSTRUCTION</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Where floor flatness is critical use paragraph FLAT FLOOR FINISHES. Coordinate concrete finish with applicable 
architectural finish material to be installed over concrete floor. For thin-set tile, coordinate with Section 
<SRF><pre class="display_SRF">&lt;SRF&gt;</pre>09 30 10<pre class="display_SRF">&lt;/SRF&gt;</pre></SRF> CERAMIC, QUARRY, AND GLASS TILING<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>In accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>JASS 5<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> and <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>MLIT-SS Chapter 6<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>, unless otherwise specified. Slope floors uniformly to drains where drains are provided.<div class="brackets">[ Depress 
the concrete base slab where quarry tile, ceramic tile, <div class="brackets">[or]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> are indicated.]</div><div class="brackets">[ Steel trowel and fine-broom finish concrete slabs that are 
to receive quarry tile, ceramic tile, or paver tile <div class="brackets">[_____]</div>.]</div> Where straightedge measurements are specified, Contractor must provide straightedge.</TXT><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.10.1"><TTL>Finish</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Place, consolidate, and immediately strike off concrete to obtain proper contour, grade, and elevation before bleedwater appears. Permit concrete 
to attain a set sufficient for floating and supporting the weight of the finisher and equipment. If bleedwater is present prior to floating the 
surface, drag the excess water off or remove by absorption with porous materials. Do not use dry cement to absorb bleedwater.</TXT><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.10.1.1"><TTL>Scratched</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Use for surfaces intended to receive bonded applied cementitious applications. Finish concrete in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 5 for a scratched 
finish.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.10.1.2"><TTL>Floated</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Use for <div class="brackets">[surfaces to receive <div class="brackets">[roofing,]</div> <div class="brackets">[waterproofing membranes,]</div> <div class="brackets">[sand bed terrazzo,]</div>]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> <div class="brackets">[and]</div> <div class="brackets">[exterior slabs where not otherwise specified.]</div> 
Finish concrete in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 5 for a floated finish.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.10.1.3"><TTL>Steel Troweled</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: ACI 302.1R suggests power troweling three times for Class 5 floors and where increased wear resistance 
is needed.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Use for floors intended as walking surfaces<div class="brackets">[,]</div> <div class="brackets">[and]</div> for reception of floor coverings<div class="brackets">[, and]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div>. Finish concrete in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>
 Section 5 for a steel troweled finish.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<div class="brackets">[<SPT outline="3.10.1.4"><TTL>Nonslip Finish</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Include when nonslip finish using dry shake aggregate is desired.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT>Use on surfaces of exterior platforms, steps, and landings; and on exterior and interior pedestrian ramps. Finish concrete in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>
ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 5 for a dry-shake finish. After the selected material has been embedded by the two floatings, complete the operation with a <div class="brackets">[broomed]</div> 
<div class="brackets">[floated]</div> <div class="brackets">[troweled]</div> finish.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
]</div><SPT outline="3.10.1.5"><TTL>Broomed</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Use on surfaces of exterior walks, platforms, patios, and ramps, unless otherwise indicated. Finish concrete in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 
5 for a broomed finish.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.10.1.6"><TTL>Pavement</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Screed the concrete with a template advanced with a combined longitudinal and crosswise motion. Maintain a slight surplus of concrete ahead of 
the template. After screeding, float the concrete longitudinally. Use a straightedge to check slope and flatness; correct and refloat as necessary. 
Obtain final finish by <div class="brackets">[belting. Lay belt flat on the concrete surface and advance with a sawing motion; continue until a uniform but gritty nonslip 
surface is obtained.]</div> <div class="brackets">[a burlap drag. Drag a strip of clean, wet burlap from<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 900 to 3000 mm wide and 600 mm longer<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 3 to 10 feet wide and 2 feet 
longer<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> than the pavement width across the slab. Produce a fine, granular, sandy textured surface without disfiguring marks.]</div> Round edges and 
joints with an edger having a radius of<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 3 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1/8 inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.10.1.7"><TTL>Chemical-Hardener Treatment</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Slab surfaces requiring a chemical hardener must be indicated. Such treatment is suitable for surfaces 
of concrete floors in equipment rooms and on other floor surfaces that are subject to light foot traffic only 
and must not be covered with resilient flooring, paint, or other finish coating.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<div class="brackets">[<TXT>Apply liquid-chemical floor hardener where indicated after curing and drying concrete surface. Dilute liquid hardener with water and apply in 
three coats. First coat must be one-third strength, second coat one-half strength, and third coat two-thirds strength. Apply each coat evenly 
and allow to dry 24 hours between coats.</TXT><BRK />
<TXT>Approved proprietary chemical hardeners must be applied in accordance with manufacturer's printed directions.</TXT><BRK />
]</div></SPT></SPT><SPT outline="3.10.2"><TTL>Flat Floor Finishes</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: Use these paragraphs where floor flatness is critical. Indicate areas where these requirements apply. 
Flatness affects the appearance and function of finishes applied to the concrete and in situations such as large 
or long expanses of glossy floor materials. Low tolerance for product (for example thin set tile and wood gymnasium 
floors) and equipment dictates to the designer to specify higher than normal flatness requirements. The numbers 
provided in brackets are typical numbers, but A/E should research and select F numbers high enough to get desired 
results but not so high as to cause undue cost increases and construction problems. Ff/FL 20/15 is equivalent 
to<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 8 mm in 5.05 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 5/16 inches in 10 feet<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>. This test method is not suitable for unshored deck. Fitted partitions 
need FL greater than or equal to 25.<BRK /><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR>
<BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>The Japanese contractors would likely not be familiar with Ff/Fl values, but would be familiar with flatness specified 
as 8mm in 5m since JASS 5 Table 2.2 specifies evenness in a similar manner. Where floor flatness is critical, 
provide description of flatness and levelness in terms familiar to Japanese contractors where possible.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>When specifying floors where flatness is important, adhere primarily to good concrete fundamentals, including 
equalizing hydration on top and bottom, reducing shrinkage prone cement paste content, and paying attention to 
curing protocol (slower is better).<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<TXT><RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 302.1R<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>. Construct in accordance with one of the methods recommended in Table 7.15.3, "Typical Composite Ff/FL Values for Various Construction 
Methods." <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 117<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> for tolerance tested by <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ASTM E1155<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>.</TXT><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Specified Conventional Value:</LST><BRK />
<ITM>Floor Flatness (Ff) <div class="brackets">[20]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> <div class="brackets">[13]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> minimum</ITM><BRK />
<ITM>Floor Levelness (FL) <div class="brackets">[15]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> <div class="brackets">[10]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> minimum</ITM><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Specified Industrial:</LST><BRK />
<ITM>Floor Flatness (Ff) <div class="brackets">[30]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> <div class="brackets">[15]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> minimum</ITM><BRK />
<ITM>Floor Levelness (FL) <div class="brackets">[20]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> <div class="brackets">[10]</div> <div class="brackets">[_____]</div> minimum</ITM><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.10.2.1"><TTL>Measurement of Floor Tolerances</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Test slab within 24 hours of the final troweling. Provide tests to Contracting Officer within 12 hours after collecting the data. Floor flatness 
inspector is required to provide a <SUB><pre class="display_SUB">&lt;SUB&gt;</pre>tolerance report<pre class="display_SUB">&lt;/SUB&gt;</pre></SUB> which must include:</TXT><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Key plan showing location of data collected.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Results required by <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ASTM E1155<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID>.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.10.2.2"><TTL>Remedies for Out of Tolerance Work</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Contractor is required to repair and retest any floors not meeting specified tolerances. Prior to repair, Contractor must submit and receive approval 
for the proposed repair, including product data from any materials proposed. Repairs must not result in damage to structural integrity of the 
floor. For floors exposed to public view, repairs must prevent any uneven or unusual coloring of the surface.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.10.3"><TTL>Concrete Walks</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Provide<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 100 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 4 inches<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> thick minimum unless otherwise indicated. Provide contraction joints spaced every<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 1500 lineal mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 5 linear feet<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> unless 
otherwise indicated. the surface has been finished. Provide<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 13 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 0.5 inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> thick transverse expansion joints at changes in direction where sidewalk abuts curb, steps, 
rigid pavement, or other similar structures; space expansion joints every<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 15 m<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 50 feet<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> maximum. Give walks a broomed finish. Unless indicated 
otherwise, provide a transverse slope of 1/48. Limit variation in cross section to<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 6 mm in 1500 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1/4 inch in 5 feet<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>

<TXT>Place bottoms and walls monolithically or provide waterstops and keys.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>

]</div></SPT><SPT outline="3.11"><TTL>JOINTS</TTL><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.11.1"><TTL>Construction Joints</TTL><BRK />
<TXT>Make and locate joints not indicated so as not to impair strength and appearance of the structure, as approved. Joints must be perpendicular to 
main reinforcement. Reinforcement must be continued and developed across construction joints. Locate construction joints as follows:</TXT><BRK />
<SPT outline="3.11.1.1"><TTL>Maximum Allowable Construction Joint Spacing</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. In walls at not more than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 18.0 meter<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 60 feet<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> in any horizontal direction.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. In slabs on ground, so as to divide slab into areas not in excess of<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> <BRK />
110 square meter<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1,200 square feet<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG>.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.11.1.2"><TTL>Construction Joints for Constructability Purposes</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. In walls, at top of footing; at top of slabs on ground; at top and bottom of door and window openings or where required to conform 
to architectural details; and at underside of deepest beam or girder framing into wall.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. In columns or piers, at top of footing; at top of slabs on ground; and at underside of deepest beam or girder framing into column or 
pier.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Near midpoint of spans for supported slabs, beams, and girders unless a beam intersects a girder at the center, in which case construction 
joints in girder must offset a distance equal to twice the width of the beam. Make transfer of shear through construction joint by use 
of inclined reinforcement.</LST><BRK />
<TXT>Provide keyways at least<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 40 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1-1/2-inches<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> deep in construction joints in walls and slabs and between walls and footings; approved bulkheads may 
be used for slabs.</TXT><BRK /></SPT>
</SPT><SPT outline="3.11.2"><TTL>Isolation Joints in Slabs on Ground</TTL><BRK />
<NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
<NPR><pre class="display_NPR">&lt;NPR&gt;</pre>NOTE: If inserts are to be used for slab on ground contraction joint use bracketed paragraph and remove paragraph 
related to sawcut joints.<pre class="display_NPR">&lt;/NPR&gt;</pre></NPR><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK /><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;/NTE&gt;</pre></NTE>
<BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Provide joints at points of contact between slabs on ground and vertical surfaces, such as column pedestals, foundation walls, grade 
beams, and elsewhere as indicated.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Fill joints with premolded joint filler strips<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 13 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1/2 inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> thick, extending full slab depth. Install filler strips at proper level 
below finish floor elevation with a slightly tapered, dress-and-oiled wood strip temporarily secured to top of filler strip to form a groove 
not less than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 20 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 3/4 inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> in depth where joint is sealed with sealing compound and not less than<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 6 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1/4 inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> in depth where joint 
sealing is not required. Remove wood strip after concrete has set. Contractor must clean groove of foreign matter and loose particles 
after surface has dried.</LST><BRK /></SPT>
<SPT outline="3.11.3"><TTL>Contraction Joints in Slabs on Ground</TTL><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">a. Provide joints to form panels as indicated.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">b. Under and on exact line of each control joint, cut 50 percent of welded wire reinforcement before placing concrete.</LST><BRK />
<LST INDENT="-0.33">c. Sawcut contraction joints into slab on ground in accordance with <RID><pre class="display_RID">&lt;RID&gt;</pre>ACI 301<pre class="display_RID">&lt;/RID&gt;</pre></RID> Section 5.</LST><BRK />
<div class="brackets">[<LST INDENT="-0.33">d. Joints must be<MET><pre class="display_MET">&lt;MET&gt;</pre> 4 mm<pre class="display_MET">&lt;/MET&gt;</pre></MET><ENG><pre class="display_ENG">&lt;ENG&gt;</pre> 1/8-inch<pre class="display_ENG">&lt;/ENG&gt;</pre></ENG> wide by 1/5 to 1/4 of slab depth and formed by inserting hand-pressed fiberboard strip into fresh concrete 
until top surface of strip is flush with slab surface. After concrete has cured for at least 7 days, the Contractor must remove inserts 
and clean groove of foreign matter and loose particles.</LST><BRK />
]</div><NTE><pre class="display_NTE">&lt;NTE&gt;</pre><BRK />
<AST><hr></AST><BRK />
